                <div class="sl-block" data-block-type="text" style="width: 1612px; left: 154px; top: 292px; height: auto;">
                    <div class="sl-block-content" style="z-index: 10;">
                        <h1>Waffle House</h1>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="sl-block" data-block-type="text" style="width: 1612px; left: 154px; top: 355px; height: auto;">
                    <div class="sl-block-content" style="z-index: 11;">
                        <ul>
                            <li>1967 locations across the U.S. (mostly in the South)</li>
                            <li>FEMA revealed in early 2010s that their disaster mobilization used the Waffle House Index as a guide
                                <ul>
                                    <li>Green - Waffle House serving full menu, open (most usually 24/7, 365)</li>
                                    <li>Yellow - Waffle House serving limited menu</li>
                                    <li>Red - Waffle House closed</li>
                                </ul>
                            </li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="sl-block" data-block-type="image" style="width: 565.646px; height: 415.184px; left: 291.128px; top: 569.401px; min-width: 1px; min-height: 1px;" data-name="image-a249c4">

                </div>
                <div class="sl-block" data-block-type="image" style="width: 566.493px; height: 415.806px; left: 1016.78px; top: 569.401px; min-width: 1px; min-height: 1px;" data-name="image-1e20a9">
                    <div class="sl-block-content" style="z-index: 13;"><img data-natural-width="1500" data-natural-height="1101" style="" data-lazy-loaded="" data-src="https://image.shutterstock.com/z/stock-photo-jacksonville-fl-may-a-waffle-house-in-jacksonville-waffle-house-inc-is-a-restaurant-194226389.jpg"></div>
                </div>

                        <h1>country</h1>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </section>
            <section>
                <div class="sl-block" data-block-type="text" data-name="text-7d1dc3" style="height: auto; width: 600px; left: 384.122px; top: 396px;">
                    <div class="sl-block-content" style="z-index: 11;">
                        <ul>
                            <li>You probably already know about pandas if you do data manipulation in python</li>
                            <li>Highly recommend revisiting their docs! A beautiful change coinciding with v1.0!
                                <ul>
                                    <li>0.25 to 1.0 is not a monumental shift, mostly a better reflection that pandas is pretty stable</li>
                                    <li>one of the best changes:
                                        <ul>
                                            <li>if you have a missing value in a column of integers when reading in to pandas, the column no longer gets cast to a float!!</li>
                                        </ul>
                                    </li>
                                    <li>more info:</li>
                                </ul>
                            </li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="sl-block sl-block-group" data-block-type="group" data-name="group-bbc6bb" style="width: auto; height: auto;">
                    <div class="sl-block-content sl-block-group-content" style="transform-origin: 951.913px 246.266px; z-index: 12;">
                        <div class="sl-block" data-block-type="text" style="width: 308.707px; left: 681.752px; top: 214.766px; height: auto;">
                            <div class="sl-block-content" style="z-index: 13; color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
                                <h1>peppered</h1>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="sl-block" data-block-type="text" style="width: 247.789px; left: 974.286px; top: 214.766px; height: auto;" data-name="text-8c02b1">
                            <div class="sl-block-content" style="z-index: 14;">
                                <h1>: Pandas</h1>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                    <div class="sl-block-content" style="z-index: 15;"><iframe webkitallowfullscreen="" mozallowfullscreen="" allowfullscreen="" sandbox="allow-forms allow-scripts allow-popups allow-same-origin allow-pointer-lock allow-presentation" data-preload="true" data-lazy-loaded="" data-src="https://pandas.pydata.org/docs/"></iframe></div>

                    <div class="sl-block-content" style="z-index: 16;">
                        <p><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/whats-new-in-pandas-1-0-ffa99bd43a58" target="_blank">https://towardsdatascience.com/whats-new-in-pandas-1-0-ffa99bd43a58</a></p>

            </section>
            <section>
                <div class="sl-block" data-block-type="text" data-name="text-7d1dc3" style="height: auto; width: 600px; left: 462.707px; top: 422.154px;">
                    <div class="sl-block-content" style="z-index: 11;">
                        <ul>
                            <li>Powerful tool in python that wraps a lot of lower level python libraries to quickly work with data that has a spatial component, think Pandas + a column for geometry</li>
                            <li>Not only can do you data joins, but you can also do geographical transformations (thanks to the underlying libraries), that can make it a useful part of your GIS stack</li>
                            <li>I won't cover the bigger geography tools, for a better dive with an actual geographer, check out KnoxData's talk with Dr. Paulo Raposo from Sept 2018 -&gt;</li>
                            <li>docs: <a href="https://geopandas.org/" target="_blank">https://geopandas.org/</a>
                            </li>
                        </ul>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="sl-block" data-block-type="iframe" data-name="iframe-ee90ba" style="width: 679.699px; height: 379.56px; left: 1160.3px; top: 422.154px;">
